# Test Report

Time: 2024-03-30 01:37:31.305001

### Base Program

```py
def numberOfWays(numPeople: int) -> int:
    MOD = 1000000007
    dp = [0] * (numPeople // 2 + 1)
    dp[0] = 1
    for i in range(1, numPeople // 2 + 1):
        for j in range(1, i + 1):
            dp[i] = (dp[i] + dp[i - j] * dp[j - 1]) % MOD
    return dp[numPeople // 2]
```

### Input

```json
[50]
```

<details>
<summary>Parser Result: Passed ✅</summary>

Message: 
```
Success
```

## Test Case 1

### Modified Program

```py
def numberOfWays(numPeople: int) -> int:
    MOD = 1000000007
    dp = [0] * (numPeople // 2 + 1)
    dp[0] = 1
    for i in range(1, numPeople // 2 + 1):
        for j in range(1, i + 1):
            dp[i] = (dp[i] + dp[i - j] * dp[j - 1]) % MOD
    return dp[numPeople // 2]
```

## Test Case 2

### Modified Program

```py
def numberOfWays(var_0: int) -> int:
    MOD = 1000000007
    dp = [0] * (var_0 // 2 + 1)
    dp[0] = 1
    for i in range(1, var_0 // 2 + 1):
        for j in range(1, i + 1):
            dp[i] = (dp[i] + dp[i - j] * dp[j - 1]) % MOD
    return dp[var_0 // 2]
```

## Test Case 3

### Modified Program

```py
def numberOfWays(numPeople: int) -> int:
    MOD = 1000000007
    dp = (1 + numPeople // 2) * [0]
    dp[0] = 1
    for i in range(1, 1 + numPeople // 2):
        for j in range(1, 1 + i):
            dp[i] = (dp[j + -1] * dp[i + -j] + dp[i]) % MOD
    return dp[numPeople // 2]
```

<details>
<summary>parser endpoint: passed ✅</summary>

```
Success
```

## Test Case 4

### Modified Program

```py
def numberOfWays(var_1: int) -> int:
    MOD = 1000000007
    dp = (1 + var_1 // 2) * [0]
    dp[0] = 1
    for i in range(1, 1 + var_1 // 2):
        for j in range(1, 1 + i):
            dp[i] = (dp[j + -1] * dp[i + -j] + dp[i]) % MOD
    return dp[var_1 // 2]
```

<details>
<summary>parser endpoint: passed ✅</summary>

